name:Pâ€eâ€nâ€gâ€yâ€uâ€yâ€aâ€nâ€dâ€eâ€bâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€mâ€eâ€i
info:Deluxe King Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Friends
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 16, 2023
msg:As a travel expert, I have stayed in many hotels across the country. This time I came to Haimen to attend a relative's wedding. I booked this hotel online. The online reviews were pretty good. I chose this hotel with the attitude of giving it a try.
First, the hotel training is very thorough. The reservation depar**ent called me to ask about my housing requirements before I checked in. They also reminded me that travel is peak during the holidays and that I should be careful on the road because there may be traffic jams. Parking at the hotel is very inconvenient. First of all, the road signs are not clear and it is easy to go in the wrong direction. Secondly, it should be because the hotel's business is so good that it is difficult to find a parking space. However, the security guard was responsible and guided me to a parking space not far from the hotel.
Secondly, there is no tall and handsome doorman in the hotel. The one who carries the luggage is actually a skinny girl. It seems that the hotel is short of people now!
Third, the room facilities are a bit outdated, the room hygiene is okay, and the service staff are also quite enthusiastic.
Fourth, the breakfast is average: no local characteristics, many pre-made products, and the noodles cooked on site have a bad taste.
In short, Donghengsheng is still a very good hotel, but some aspects still need to be improved.
